   BhG 4.1	Bhu 4.1
   śrī-bhagavān uvāca	SrI--BagavAn uvAca

   śrīdharaḥ :	SrIDaraH :

   paśyati sa paśyati [Gītā 5.6] ity anayā diśā sādhya-sādhanayoḥ phalaikyād	paSyati sa paSyati [GItA 5.6] iti anayA diSA sADya--sADanayoH Pala-EkyAt-
   aikyam upacarya sādhana-bhūtaṃ karma-yogaṃ sādhya-bhūtaṃ ca jñāna-yogam	Ekyam upacarya sADana--BUtam karma--yogam sADya--BUtam ca jQAna--yogam

   bhāvaḥ |	BAvaH |

   avyayaṃ nityaṃ vedārtahtvān naveyeti sva-phalādityavyabhicāri-phalatvāc ca	avyayam nityam veda-ArtahtvAt naveyA-iti sva---Pala-Aditya-vyaBicAri--Pala-tvAt ca

   BhG 4.2	Bhu 4.2
   evaṃ paramparā-prāptam imaṃ rājarṣayo viduḥ |	evam paramparA--prAptam imam rAjarzayaH viduH |

   nimi-pramukhāḥ | sva-pitrādibhir ikṣvāku-pramukhaiḥ protkam imaṃ yogam	nimi--pramuKAH | sva-pitR-AdiBiH ikzvAku--pramuKEH protkam imam yogam

   vicchinna-sampradāyo jātaḥ | taṃ vinā puruṣārthāprāpter aho daurbhāgyaṃ	vicCinna--sampradAyaH jAtaH | tam vinA puruza-arTa-aprApteH aho dOrBAgyam

   śatru-gaṇaṃ śauryeṇa balavatā vivekena tapasā ca bhānur iva tāpayatīti	Satru--gaNam SOryeNa balavatA vivekena tapasA ca BAnuH iva tApayati-iti
   parantapaḥ śatru-tāpano jitendriya ity arthaḥ |	parantapaH Satru-tApanaH jita-indriyaH iti arTaH |

   BhG 4.3	Bhu 4.3

   samāna-vayāḥ snigdha-sahāyo 'si sarvadā bhavasi atas tubhyam ukta ity	samAna--vayAH snigDa--sahAyaH asi sarvadA Bavasi atas tuByam uktaH iti-
   arthaḥ anyasmai kuto nocyate tatrāha | hi yasmād etaj jñānam uttamaṃ	arTaH anyasmE kutas na-ucyate tatra-Aha | hi yasmAt etat jQAnam uttamam
   rahasyam atigopyam ||3||	rahasyam ati-gopyam ||3||

   bhāva-dvayam | anyas tu arvācīnaṃ praty eva avaktavyatve hetū rahasyam iti	BAva--dvayam | anyaH tu arvAcInam prati eva avaktavya-tve hetuH rahasyam iti
   baladevaḥ : sa eva tadānupūrvika-vacana-vācyo yogo mayā	baladevaH : saH eva tad-AnupUrvika-vacana--vAcyaH yogaH mayA

   bhaktaḥ prapannaḥ sakhā cāsīti hetor na tv anyasmai kasmaicit | tatra	BaktaH prapannaH saKA ca-asi-iti hetoH na tu anyasmE kasmEcid | tatra
   hetuḥ rahasyam iti | hi yasmād uttamaṃ rahasyam iti gopyam etat ||3||	hetuH rahasyam iti | hi yasmAt uttamam rahasyam iti gopyam etat ||3||
   BhG 4.4	Bhu 4.4
   arjuna uvāca	arjunaH uvAca
